            <div class="ds-overview-section">
             <div class="Text-c11n-8-37-1__aiai24-0 sc-pzLqt fnYwkq">
              Stunning 2 bedroom condo overlooking the iconic fountain in historic Old Louisville! This spacious 3rd floor condo was completely remodeled in 2019 and boasts impressive views, state of the art kitchen, vibrant new paint, and modern lighting. The living space feels luxurious without sacrificing the charm you would expect in a home from this era. The first thing you will notice upon entering the home is the abundance of natural light spilling into each room through the newly restored windows. All new storm windows were installed and are fully operational. Brand new Roman shades and appropriate pulls were constructed of fabric from California and installed to cover all of the windows, New screen and storm doors were installed front and back. A new faux coal gas operated fixture was installed in the fireplace creating a warm, cozy environment. A state of the art kitchen, double in size from the original with state of the art appliances, including a subzero fridge, a Cove dishwasher, a Wolf stove with the signature red knobs and convection oven, a Miele built-in espresso/cappucino/latte/coffee machine, a Miele built in microwave/convection oven, and a wine cooler. The floor to ceiling drawers and cabinets with a variation of sizes and pull out shelving maximize the space and allow for plenty of storage. Accent lighting has been installed under the cabinets for an extra touch of class. In the bathroom you will find a new sink/vanity unit, a Japanese toilet, a new shower, and new outlets and lighting. The electric in the unit has been updated where necessary and is self-contained. New chandeliers were installed in every room and recessed lighting was installed in the corridor. New matching lighting was installed in every closet. New light switches with a dimmer option were installed throughout the home. There is plenty of space and modern amenities to operate a home office (or two) and potentially a home classroom in this unit. No expense was spared on this renovation! The HOA has recently painted the exterior of the unit. You will find a shared balcony in the rear of the home and there is a storage unit in the basement of the building. Easily one of the most impressive features of this home is the top floor balcony overlooking the fountain on St. James Ct. Imagine relaxing here daily taking in the scenery! The building is rich in history, dating back to 1897. It was built by Theopholis Conrad and is claimed to be the first apartment house in Louisville. Prominent past residents have included Abraham Flexner, an educator with a profound influence on medical education (1904-1905) and Julian "Pappy" Van Winkle, who was secretary of distillers at W.L. Weller &amp; Sons (1911). Don't miss this opportunity to call this place home - schedule a private showing today!

             About GreatSchools
            </h5>
            <div>
             <p class="Text-c11n-8-37-1__aiai24-0 iuKPve">
              The GreatSchools Summary Rating is based on several metrics.
             </p>
             <div class="text-fold-container">
              <div class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap">
               <div class="attribution">
                <p class="Text-c11n-8-37-1__aiai24-0 iuKPve">
                 <strong>
                  About the ratings:
                 </strong>
                 GreatSchools Ratings are designed to be a starting point to help parents compare schools, and should not be the only factor used in selecting the right school for your family. Zillow and GreatSchools recommend that parents tour multiple schools in-person to inform that choice. As of October 2020, the GreatSchools Ratings methodology continues to move beyond proficiency and standardized test scores. The latest methodology prioritizes student growth through measures of equity and school quality.
                 <a href="http://www.greatschools.org/gk/ratings/" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
                  <!-- -->
                  Learn more
                 </a>
                </p>

                  Disclaimer:
                 </strong>
                 School attendance zone boundaries are provided by a third party and are subject to change. They are not guaranteed to be accurate, up to date, or complete. Check with the applicable school district prior to making a decision based on these boundaries.
